<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/1/Pages/21451.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 21451&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_session.txt(This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and Workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/adm/syslog/syslog.log file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; href=&quot;#23b14880-40fe-11e5-bcfa-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bfc08e30-4fe9-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;abdd9260-4fe8-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;AIX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to the&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166937.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt; KB 166937&amp;nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;to see the options and possible reasons for no core file.      </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;debugger-used&amp;gt; &lt;strong&gt;eg pmstack -c core.1234 -d dbx&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#8de57c80-4cca-11e5-8d3f-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#abdd9260-4fe8-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back8de57c80-4cca-11e5-8d3f-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#abdd9260-4fe8-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;3d7302f0-4fe9-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Windows&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs&lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt; Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Crashes do not generate system level dumps by default on Windows. It is recommended to configure debugDiag on the crashing process to get system level dumps. Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/whitepapers/4/Pages/1/522617.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 522617&lt;/a&gt; to configure debugDiag on the server to monitor processes and generate dumps in case of a crash.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Output of the following command from the server:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166689.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166689&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.           </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_session.txt (This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/log/messages file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#44f6a880-4fec-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#2c8471d0-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back44f6a880-4fec-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#2c8471d0-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166689.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166689&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.           </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_session.txt (This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/log/messages file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166931&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to see the options and possible reasons for no core file.      </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#a0ad89d0-4fe9-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7b160a40-473c-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa0ad89d0-4fe9-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#7b160a40-473c-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs&lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt; Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Crashes do not generate system level dumps by default on Windows. It is recommended to configure debugDiag on the crashing process to get system level dumps. Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/whitepapers/4/Pages/1/522617.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 522617&lt;/a&gt; to configure debugDiag on the server to monitor processes and generate dumps in case of a crash.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166931&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.        </div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_session.txt (This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/adm/messages file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to the&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166937.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt; KB 166937&amp;nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;to see the options and possible reasons for no core file.      </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;debugger-used&amp;gt; &lt;strong&gt;eg pmstack -c core.1234 -d dbx&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs&lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;d6d7da00-4fea-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;AIX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166937.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166937&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;debugger-used&amp;gt; &lt;strong&gt;eg pmstack -c core.1234 -d dbx&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jextract &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; jextract_core(This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Output of the following command from the server       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;errpt -a &amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;errpr_aix.txt&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs. &lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Crashes do not generate system level dumps by default on Windows. It is recommended to configure debugDiag on the crashing process to get system level dumps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/whitepapers/4/Pages/1/522617.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 522617&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to configure debugDiag on the server to monitor processes and generate dumps in case of a crash. You need to monitor the pmdtm process in a session crash issue.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;HP-UX&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#494abd30-4fe8-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#be3f2e60-4722-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back494abd30-4fe8-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#be3f2e60-4722-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/supporttv/1/Pages/1/302483.aspx?docid=302483&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=5&amp;amp;myk=infa9Logs&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for information on how to collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following command on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/1/Pages/21451.aspx?docid=21451&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=2&amp;amp;myk=no%20core%20file%20created%20amita&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 21451&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to see the other options and possible reasons for no core file creation.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_core.txt&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;libscollector&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/1/Pages/21451.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;hs_err_pid*&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;*.hprof&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;files under the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(&lt;em&gt;/var/adm/syslog/syslog.log&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;file).&amp;nbsp;The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#4ca29ac0-4fe8-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#be3f2e60-4722-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back4ca29ac0-4fe8-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#be3f2e60-4722-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/supporttv/1/Pages/1/302483.aspx?docid=302483&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=5&amp;amp;myk=infa9Logs&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for information on how to collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following command on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/1/Pages/21451.aspx?docid=21451&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=2&amp;amp;myk=no%20core%20file%20created%20amita&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 21451&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to see the other options and possible reasons for no core file creation.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_core.txt&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;libscollector&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/1/Pages/21451.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;hs_err_pid*&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;*.hprof&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;files under the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(&lt;em&gt;/var/adm/syslog/syslog.log&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;file).&amp;nbsp;The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs. &lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Crashes do not generate system level dumps by default on Windows. It is recommended to configure debugDiag on the crashing process to get system level dumps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/whitepapers/4/Pages/1/522617.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 522617&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to configure debugDiag on the server to monitor processes and generate dumps in case of a crash. You need to monitor the pmdtm process in a session crash issue.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#417dd570-4fec-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#29762060-473e-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back417dd570-4fec-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#29762060-473e-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Event logs. &lt;br /&gt;Obtain these from the Windows &lt;em&gt;Event viewer&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;Save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; Application&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Windows Logs &amp;gt; System&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Crashes do not generate system level dumps by default on Windows. It is recommended to configure debugDiag on the crashing process to get system level dumps.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/whitepapers/4/Pages/1/522617.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 522617&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to configure debugDiag on the server to monitor processes and generate dumps in case of a crash. You need to monitor the pmdtm process in a session crash issue.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back29762060-473e-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#29762060-473e-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#23b14880-40fe-11e5-bcfa-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#29762060-473e-11e5-a700-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;a32cec40-4fea-11e5-bdb0-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Solaris&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166931&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_session.txt (This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and Workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/adm/messages file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did you face any issues while collecting the above?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;The core file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;javacore.*, Snap.*, *.phd &lt;/em&gt;files under the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Output of the following command from the server:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166931.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166931&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to see the options and possible reasons for no core file.      </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166689.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166689&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.           </div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration Service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(/var/log/messages file). The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#174ac380-4fec-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#377d9670-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back174ac380-4fec-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#377d9670-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166937.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166937&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;debugger-used&amp;gt; &lt;strong&gt;eg pmstack -c core.1234 -d dbx&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run libscollector on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jextract &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; jextract_core(This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow XML exported from Repository Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Output of the following command from the server       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;errpt -a &amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;errpr_aix.txt&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#4c397be0-4fec-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#377d9670-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back4c397be0-4fec-11e5-8deb-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#377d9670-473e-11e5-b4bf-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following commands on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/&lt;/em&gt; directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166937.aspx&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166937&lt;/a&gt; to see the options.        </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;debugger-used&amp;gt; &lt;strong&gt;eg pmstack -c core.1234 -d dbx&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;jextract &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; jextract_core(This step is only applicable is the session has a Java transformation)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Repository service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Integration service logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Session and workflow logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;hs_err_pid*&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;*.hprof&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;files under the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(&lt;em&gt;/var/adm/messages&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;file).&amp;nbsp;The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#fceeb450-4fe7-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b685cb70-4722-11e5-9f08-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backfceeb450-4fe7-11e5-978a-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#b685cb70-4722-11e5-9f08-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Collect the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/supporttv/1/Pages/1/302483.aspx?docid=302483&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=5&amp;amp;myk=infa9Logs&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information on how to collect &lt;em&gt;infa9Logs&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you find a core file generated for the crash, run the following command on the core file and share the output. Usually, the file would be generated in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory, if not, refer to &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/faq/7/Pages/4/166931.aspx?docid=166931&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=4&amp;amp;myk=core%20file%20not%20generated&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;KB 166931&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to see the other options and possible reasons for no core file creation.      </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;pmstack -c&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;jstack &amp;lt;core-file-name&amp;gt; &amp;gt; jstack_core.txt&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;libscollector&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;on the core file. Click &lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/howto/3/Pages/144522.aspx?docid=144522&amp;amp;type=internal&amp;amp;index=3&amp;amp;myk=libscollector&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; for more information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;hs_err_pid*&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;*.hprof&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;files under the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/tomcat/bin/&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain logs&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;System logs(&lt;em&gt;/var/adm/messages&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;file).&amp;nbsp;The file requires root privileges.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
